vector space ^O2OxHm6G

let V be a set w. vector addition and scalar multiplication defined. if foreach u,v ^ w e V ^ foreach c ^ d e R the following are true ⟶ V is a vector space ^d8Xb6avs

associative ^2ouHfdOr

distributive ^rqFsPCC8

E zero vector e V s.t. 0+u=u+0=u, foreach u e V ^oUwgY0za

E -u e V s.t. u+(-u)=-u+u=0 ^JXmkyiOe

1u=u ^1lBf7Jco

c(du)=(cd)u ^WAqPePVA

(c+d)u=cu+du ^QRfkeWQF

classic ^icEnr1oG

not necessarily a set of tuples ^blqQlAFH

not always ^w2y0oauR
